<script type="text/javascript">
    (function (global, undefined) {
        function setCookieWithTime(name, value, time/*单位天*/) {//设置cookies
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + time * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
            document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) + ";expires=" + date.toGMTString();
        }
        function setCookieTips() {
            if (oCookie.getCookie('if_zfb_tip') && oCookie.getCookie('if_zfb_tip') == 1)
                return false;
            setCookieWithTime('if_zfb_tip', '1', 1);
        }
        $("#new_alipay_tip,#new_alipay_not").on('click', function (evt) {
            setCookieTips();
            clearTimeout('timer1');
            clearTimeout('timer2');
            $(this).css('display', 'none');
        });
        var oUserInfo = oCookie.getCookie('_user', true);
        if (!oUserInfo) return;
        oUserInfo = JSON.parse(oUserInfo);
        var nick = oUserInfo['nick'] || '';
        var alipay = oUserInfo['alipay'] || '';
        nick = nick.length > 10 ? nick.slice(0, 10) + ".." : nick;
        if (!oCookie.getCookie('if_zfb_tip') || oCookie.getCookie('if_zfb_tip') != 1) {
            if (alipay.length > 0) {
                $('#new_alipay_tip').show();
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $('#new_alipay_tip').hide();
                }, 6000);
            }else {
                $('#new_alipay_not').show();
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $('#new_alipay_not').hide();
                }, 6000);
            }
        }
        $('#login_st_hi').html('Hi， ' + nick + '&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;');
    })(window);
</script>
